2026-07-16 | Fire 77 — process lesson: highest-ever single-fire scout-dedup-failure rate | KB-process note, not a finding | Of ~13 "new" candidates reported across the VC-portfolio, HKEX-A1, Korea-DART, and Chinese-trade-press scouts this fire, 9 were already-known/already-killed and caught only at orchestrator synthesis (Laifu Harmonic, KH Vatec, Robotis, Samhyun, Samgi, Global SM, ITM Semiconductor, Xinjian Transmission/Seenpin, Benmo Power) — a ~70% false-positive rate on "new" claims, matching and possibly exceeding the Fire 61 record (~72%). 2026-07-16 | Fire 80 — HSAI market-cap methodology error CAUGHT AND RE-CORRECTED (2nd time) | KB-process/data-integrity fix, not a portfolio decision | A Fire-80 price-refresh scout reproduced an already-fixed (Fire 59/74) error: computing mkt cap as 1,257,137,688 (post-split ORDINARY share count) × ADS price = $19.7B. 2026-07-18 | Hesai Group (HSAI, Nasdaq) | DOWNGRADE 7/8→~5/8 — from PARKED/armed-to-promote-to-#1 to low-conviction WATCH/monitor | This fire's staleness-guard fact-refresh (explicitly flagged as due since Fire 89's DIGEST/FRESH-ANGLES notes) pulled Hesai's own FY2025 6-K customer/segment classification directly: Hesai itself separates "ADAS" (passenger+commercial vehicles, 85.2% of FY2025 units) from "Robotics" (robotaxi+humanoid+lawn-mowers+AGVs, 14.8% of units) — and Mercedes-Benz L3, previously scored in this KB as "genuinely robotaxi/L3+-grade" (a claim from Fire 89's own catalyst scout), is actually in Hesai's OWN ADAS bucket, an ordinary passenger-vehicle consumer feature. Genuinely-qualifying robotaxi+humanoid revenue (Zoox/Motional/Pony.ai/WeRide/Baidu/DiDi + Unitree/HONOR Robot/Galbot/Magiclab/Vita Dynamics, all primary-sourced) is an estimated single-digit-to-low-teens % of total revenue, not the ~90%+ implicitly assumed by the carried 7/8 score. Bear/base/bull (qualifying-segment-driven whole-stock price): $9-12/$14-19/$28-40.
